< Review>
First Jollibee in Bakersfield I think.

Went early since my lunch hour starts real early. Lucky for me they open at 9am.

This place has been open a bit over a week and the lines during the daytime are crazy long!

But I came just as they opened so I didn‚Äôt have any problems walking up ordered my food‚Ä¶got my food‚Ä¶sat and enjoyed my lunch.

I had the Two-Piece Burger Steak with white rice eand a diet soda. And it was delicious.

The restaurant was nice and clean.

The staff was friendly and very helpful!

I would recommend coming here!!!<//Review>

<name>Brandon Decker</name><time>1542432406247< /time>< rate>
4</rate>
<text>On a good day Laroccos has good to excellent quality authentic New York style pizza. The only problem in quality control does not seem to come from the ingredients, equipment or the building so much as it does from the professionalism of the employees. I get the distinct impression oftentimes that they are there to do the absolute minimum necessary to maintain a paycheck and not be fired. My guess is that the employees are paid at a bare minimum and neither have the leadership or the financial incentive to give anything near a hundred percent.
I have been in there dozens upon dozens of times and have no clue who the manager is or who runs the restaurant. For someone who frequents larocco's as often as I do this strikes me as a little bit odd from a mom and pop style Pizzeria.
This indicates to me that the ownership has likely become very distant in their involvement in the daily operations and as a consequence Laroccos lacks the distinct personality of a family-run pizzeria.
While I certainly do not require a fat Italian with a mustache named Mario running the joint, they should have someone who is involved and who clearly cares about the customers experience above all other issues. It is intrinsic to this kind of restaurant and completely lacking.
Maybe larocco's can exist purely on its laurels but in such a state they are in my opinion much more close to losing critical mass of business then they realise. I would encourage the ownership to invest more in their employees and attempt to make larocco's the kind of place that is a desirable job rather than something for kids to satiate their parents with basic employment
To be clear this is not at all and indictment of the employees who work there. That would be like blaming a janitor for a shuttle blowing up at NASA. It is completely unreasonable to expect a wet behind the ears high school students to bring the atmosphere an experienced manager who's personally invested in the business and who has the knowledge required to consistently bring an A game on a daily basis.< /text><Pics>None< /Pics><response>None< /response><gmapID>0x80dcf46e58d7ab0b:0x20e7bd20adc6c802< /gmapID></record></dataset><record>

<text>Oh. My. God. Let me tell you a little something about LaRocco's Pizzeria, it is literally THE BEST PIZZA I HAVE EVER HAD!
Personally, I love thin crust pizza, so as soon as I took a bite into that cheese pizza, I knew that I'd never find anything like it. I also LOVEEE the garlic knotts! Carb heaven up there! I have been going the pizza joint since I was a little girl and I have never gotten sick/tired of this pizza, I could eat it for weeks!
The staff is so sweet and kind, they really do care about their customers. One time I was ordering 2 slices of cheese pizza and a soft drink and the cash register broke. One of the guys I knew was working there and he was trying to fix it for about 10 minutes. All I had was a 20 so he ended up letting me have the food and drink for free. This was so sweet! I will never forget the day that happened!
It's a very casual and family friendly joint. There's some seating in the front of the resturaunt, but most is is in the back. I normally go to the back because the front is filled up.

<rating>4< /rating>< text>
Sprouts has come a long way since the first time I entered one.

We finally went to the sprouts here in Ventura, the store is clean bright with lots of fresh food and a friendly helpful staff.
We like the fact that they always have fresh food, especially fish and the meat dept.
They have excellent sausages and they make are huge and the make some cool burger patties like feta cheddar turkey burger and a jalape√±o cheddar burger patties.

They have wild caught Salmon and not just one piece which seems to be the norm at all the other stores around here which is weird since we are right on the ocean!

The fresh fruit and veggies are on point and take up like half the store. They have a great dry goods section of nuts, fruit and trail mix.

We got a couple of sandwiches from the deli and they were stacked with meat and veggies for like 5 bucks.

The new first stop is sprouts for us. Its whats for dinner.< /text>

Just checked out the new store and I really enjoyed it! The selection is great (much better than Trader Joe's). There are so many areas with a great selection, I'll just name my highlights. Asian section: lots of sauces, pastes, noodle and rice variety. Veggies: many less common veggies available. Particularly chilis. They dont have every chili I could want, but having more than just jalape√±os is a start! Meat section is much bigger than Trader Joe's. The prices looked pretty reasonable - although I haven't done a trip yet for my weekly groceries.  The layout of the store is very open, which makes it easy to find things as well as being inviting. I hate stores that have teeny tiny aisles and induce claustrophobia...(Trader Joe's) The store was staffed very well for their second day of business. Everyone working there was super nice and seemed to have such a positive attitude. Like they were excited to be there. I had such a great experience - I hope my weekly trip is a reasonable price because I like the store a lot!</text>

My husband and I recently went to the Sprouts store @ 4870 Telephone Rd. Ventura, CA 93003 to purchase some salad dressings and Hemp Milk.They're a little pricey, but they have great products that we have not been able to find elsewhere. However, this was a horrible experience.......

My husband and I checked out at the register that Manager: Konnie was working at. Everything was seemingly fine at first. We asked her to split the bill between two cards and she said it was fine. When she ran the first card, she looked up and said, "Oh, it ran the whole amount. Well, I pressed $8.50. Have a good night, goodbye." And continued to greet the next customer. My husband then said "Excuse me....you didn't apologize or offer to fix it or anything...I find that quite rude." To which she replied in an exhausted manner, "I can refund it if you want and recharge...". My husband then brought up the point that she didn't even apologize or anything..just sort of brushed it off. We asked to speak with her manager. She replied, "I am the manager." We asked where we could make a complaint. She replied" Excuse me, I am manning the register. I will not be rude to my customer." Then proceeded to ignore us as she greeted the next person in line with a huge smile. I said "But...WE are customers as well..." She continued to ignore us. We then asked a young man close by if there was a manager we could speak to.....he pointed at Konnie. I then walked towards the vitamin section of the store, vocally asking for a manager for help.

Brett"

Stumbled upon Ten-Ichi this weekend with my friend, as we were strolling on Upper Fillmore, and I was CRAVING Japanese food. Turns out Ten-Ichi is Family owned and has been in business since the late 70's! < text>
I've dined here many times because I live in the neighborhood. I so want to love this place because of the history and proximity, but the food quality is just not good and it's gotten worse each time. I'm Japanese and when I'm too lazy to go far or cook myself, I come here to seek comfort. Fish is not fresh. One time there was plastic wrap in my sushi. Today the udon was horrible, the outside mushy and falling apart while the inside was undercooked and chalky. The broth was palatable because it's probably a solid factory made concentrate. Tempura batter was overworked and chewy. It just seems like staff in the kitchen just don't care and have no clue what good Japanese food is supposed to taste like. The servers are kind and hard-working, but because they are understaffed, presumably due to decreased business, the service is slow and patchy. Fingers crossed that this place gets the right help it needs to update its menu and improve processes to get it right.</text>

< text>
It's been a benchmark of Fresno since 1991. It's loaded with action, especially on Friday and Saturday nights.

The 1/3 and 2/5 No Limit games can have anywhere from $2000 to $5000, respectively on the table at any time (especially during a Friday and Saturday night). Their 4/8 limit Hold 'Em games are especially action packed in the evening. The action can start at 7pm and the game usually will run uninterrupted all through the night. They also have a good 8/16 limit game which will mostly run Saturday evening.

Perhaps the best limit game that Club One holds is their Omaha Hi-Lo game, which runs every evening. It may be the number one action game in the club. If you like Omaha, you should check it out.< /text>

<Text>Horrible experience at this casino. I am visiting Fresno for work and read on the reviews of this casino; I was informed this hotel was worth a visit, I was informed wrong!

The food was not bad for the price, I played a few games of blackjack, friendly dealers. I'm a big tipper and probably the only one who tipped.

The main reason I visited was for the poker, there was a wait list and only one game available, so I put my name on the list for the 1/3 no limit, after an hour into playing BlackJack they opened a new table. Great table, great players, friendly attitude, and the dealers were VERY friendly. The floor not so much. We had a great table going and our chip leader was relocated to another table which we all were upset (including him), to see him go, then when another chip leader was instructed to move he threw a fit requesting NOT to be moved, because our table had action. The floor told him he had to move or he couldn't play, so the player pulled his chips and left the game; about 5 of the players at the table commented how the action was all gone and there were no chips to play against. I was the only chipleader at the table ($480ish) - at this point I made a joke to the floor saying the table denies the move of the chipleaders to the floor (Her name was MeeMee) - at this point she told me if I had a complaint/problem I needed to step aside and address her. I told her up front it was ridiculous and defeated the purpose of most of us wanting to play because the casino (or her) was killing the action - she gave me negative attitude and said "If you don't like it don't play here," at which I commented Yelp will be hearing about my rating.

At this point she gave me an attitude and I asked her for her name, which she immediately covered it up (which of course I already knew it was MeeMee) - I told her I'm from out of town and play at other poker rooms, including Vegas and from all my experience playing over 10 years in card rooms this was by far the most unprofessional; at this point she asked me out loud for the table to hear, "If you play in Vegas, why are you playing at a $1/3 table?" which pretty much was taken as an insult, the majority of the tables, including dealer heard it and even saw it as a "low-blow." At this point 4 of the players who had a stack cashed out, and I followed there-after.

All in all, the dealers are amazing, the insult I received from the floor basically calling me "poor" on how she addressed it, was very unprofessional. I told her I wouldn't visit the casino again for the remainder of my visit in the city during the week, she basically said "GOOD." - I tipped the dealer over $75 after I cashed out proving to her how much I was there for fun, not for the money; the floor took the fun out of my visit, I rate this casino in the negative if I could...I suggest if you go, the floor will do whatever it takes to ruin your time.

Oh, and another funny thing, as soon as I picked my chips up and left she told the cashier to put a "on-break" sign on the cage...talk about a cheap casino.</Text>< rating>
